<Review>Good for cigarettes and not much else.

The floor layout is haphazard for anything else and if you are new to the place.

Asked about zippo butane fuel, which is a product produced and distributed to stores by Zippo company and the guy told me it doesn't exist and he has worked there for twenty-one years. I asked about types of pipe tobacco he sold there and he had trouble finding the several locations around the store they were hidden. That all indicates that his knowledge of his stock and the whole industry extends only as far as his cigarette counter.

I bought a different brand of butane and at the end of my transaction he said, "look around first next time." Saying that to someone unfamiliar with a store that has piss poor layout and confused store owners is a brazen example of ignoring the bottom line: repeat business.

But, if you want a pack of Marlboros and nothing else, despite what the sign out front claims (obviously there aren't "fine cigars" kept the way they should be so they don't dry out or get beetles.), then the shop is for you. <Time>1427527746235< /Time><rate>2<//rate>< review>
The restaurant looks pretty cool inside.  They have an outside bar and seating.  When we got there we asked to see the menu. The waitress told us to take a seat. We asked again if we can see the menu just to look at that they have.  She insisted we sit.  Ok fine we picked a table and she brought the menu's.  Then she brought us chips and salsa. We let her know again we are just looking at the menu on what they have if we plan to eat there.  Ok so ske left.  So we looked it over and decided ok fine a different place. The menu looks good, prices are decent, we'll stay.  So, we waited for her and nothing.  Over 5 min waiting to see if she will come check up on us. Nope, so my husband got up to get her.  Finally we ordered.  We got their Carne asada combo plate with flower tortillas and a Grande fish taco with a margarita mixed mango and fresa.  She brought the margarita which liked good with the combo plate.  The Carne asada looked a little burned,  we got corn tortillas instead so my husband took them back and asked for flower.  We sipped the margarita but no taste of mango at all. (Sigh, ok fine) so we are sharing the combo plate but where is my fish taco.  5 min later comes the flower tortillas and the fish taco. Why did a fish taco take longer then the asada Idk but cool I'm ready.  I looked at it and had to open it like what the hell is this.  It was paper thin and was burned.  I love fish tacos and looks nothing like the picture.  That was not a grande (large) fish taco. Literally the length 4 in, width 2 in and thickness 2 millimeters.  I was going to complain but I was hungry and already waited. All I know is im So Not going back. Don't mess with my fish tacos. I don't eat them much because their fried but when I do I expect a great taco. she did check up on us time to time if we needed water.  We finished and we are waiting.  10 min and where is she.  So my husband for the 3rd time got up to get her.  We got our check and the receipt said small fish taco. I asked for large. I'm glad anyways because that taco was not good. This overall experience was a "C". Now our curiosity is over about this place and not going back.< /review>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
As a Mexican pitmaster and cook I tried this spot on Sunday, we had some last minute guest and didn't have time to marinade asada or chicken so I stopped by this spot. It's a family owned business and everything is pretty much home made there. I got the asada marinated with naranja the same with the chicken and I also tried the dried longaniza and I got to say they were all great! Everyone loved it! They were grilled on mesquite lump charcoal for a real BBQ taste none of that gas grill stuff! For that person talking about asada and not being that great then sending you 200 miles up north just does not know. In Mexico asada is marinated with just salt and pepper but then here in the states there are unlimited marinades it's just personal preference with many being too overwhelming and taking away from the natural flap meat flavor. This marinade is just perfect not overpowering thank you guys this is my go to carniceria!<//review>

I had went to smile direct club back in February. I met with the sweetest person ever her name is Adrianna. We connected on a deep level. She was super generous, very accommodating and understanding. I met with other staff, but Adrianna blew me away with her generosity and character. She made me feel like I was making the right choice especially when I'm very insecure about my smile. I have to give Adrianna 5 stars! I wanted to do this review back in February, but I just kept pushing it sorry Adriana! Thank you for the best experience!

Whether you choose smile direct club, I do say you should check that out with your primary dentist first and have ur own personal X-rays because smile direct club don't actually do a deep x-ray they only get a good visual of your smile and not your jaw and beyond that which can be dangerous if  your smile needs a major fix. If its a minor fix like myself however, still get it checked out with your primary dentist check for cavities and see if smile direct club is for you.</Review>

< text>
Smile Direct Club has good marketing. The text based reminder system is impressively well polished. The iPad application they use to collect information was good except for two issues. One part had a date picker that didn‚Äôt let you change the month unless you change the year first which was non-intuitive. I‚Äôm a software engineer who makes user interfaces like these for a living and I couldn‚Äôt figure out how to make it work without assistance. The other issue was that in several places, you were expected to enter date information with the touch pad, which was very clunky. I‚Äôve never seen any software attempt to collect date information this way.

A blond woman who I assume was the general manager seemed slightly disgruntled, which seemed out of place with the customer focused image the company is trying to project, but I didn‚Äôt have to interact with her much.

The biggest issue I have to report about my experience was the demeanor of the technician who did my scan. I‚Äôm not the sort of person who requires or even likes a sappy contrived customer service persona, but I can safely say that her demeanor isn‚Äôt appropriate for a public facing role. She‚Äôd ask if I had questions, and then seemed impatient about answering them.  From the very beginning of the process, she made me feel like she didn‚Äôt like me and felt contempt towards me.
